# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="8cd9b-102">Membros obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cd9b-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8cd9b-103">As tabelas deste artigo listam os membros de tipo obsoletos no .NET Framework 4.5 e em versões posteriores, organizados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cd9b-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8cd9b-104">Use os links a seguir para ver uma lista dos membros obsoletos e as alternativas recomendadas em cada assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cd9b-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8cd9b-105">Este artigo não lista os membros de tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cd9b-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8cd9b-106">Para obter uma lista de tipos obsoletos, consulte [Tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8cd9b-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
